Great spot for a hangout .The men's restroom at this park is closed due to the repair of the re toliet. Men who are in need of a restroom stop should use the women's restroom only after asking if there any women in thereusing the restroom. Also, across the street from the park there's a women shelter and many of the women use that restroom so please be polite and courteous.The Department of Parks and Recreation takes care of the spark but but the National Park Service manages the park. Just adjacent to the restroom is a tennis c ourt and the San Francisco Department of Emergency Management and services.< /Review>

Found this small place by off chance.

They make their own ice cream and even have a vegan option as well.

The grill area is small and all the food is made to order. Their menu is small and it covers just about everything you may want to eat, as long as it comes on bread, wrapped, or a salad.

Today they were out of (3) ice cream flavors, which seems odd. If they make their own on site, why not do so on a daily basis, or if one sells out?

The service was as good as to be expected.

We only have one scoop each; Strawberry (tasted like strawberry quick) and Swiss Chip Orange (tasted like a chocolate orange; you know the one that is sold around the holiday?)</Review>

< review>
Absolutely, one of the best homemade
ice-creams & Banana Splits anywhere in our
country!  I should know, since I was an Carvel
Ice-cream store manager when I was a teen in
NYC.
Tons of flavor choices, that taste amazing!
Most choices are not made overly sweet,
but just right.
It is a hidden humble place, well known by locals
over decades.  They almost went out of business
a few years back due to an ownership change.
The locals basically "screamed for ice-cream" and
the new owners probably realized that they
had a sure thing going on.
Inside it is not fancy, but is very comfortable, with
comfy old style booths.
Besides or before you get the "required" Sundae
or BS, they do have a nice selection of dinner type
eats.  They are all quite good & made fresh.
Their service comes with lots of smiles & they are
more than happy to have you try lots of samples
as you decide what scoops to place on your BS.
Their BS is no BS!
This old school Ice-cream shop is one of few
gems in otherwise boring Modesto.  Thanks!</review>

Easily one of the best spots to photograph the Golden Gate Bridge.   You can see in all directions really well.   We were lucky to have a sunny day.  You can walk through some of the Second World War fortifications and imagine how difficult it must have been to construct what they built.  A good place to practise your hill climbing if you enjoy cycling.</Review>

discovery and exploration.
Recommend use of the National
Speleological Society for local
contact information.  American
association for the advancement
of science.  Recreation reference.
Coastal caves require access at
scheduled low tide.   Boating and
mountaineering skills might be
required.  None have installed
electric lighting and improved
access.  Enter at own risk.  Cave
area extent is Marin and San
Francisco County.  They are not
man-made.   All have daily risk
of dangerous tidal surges.   Maps
of Marin caves began to be made
in 1927.   Map-making continues.
As additional entry is found for
exploration.  Free training is available .
In USA speleology skills that include
cartography, climbing, and exploration.
From the Alabama based leadership
and regional memberships (3 of which
are amid the San Francisco Bay Area).
That was how I began in 1964.

In my opinion the Marin Headlands has the absolute best view of San Francisco. On a day when the clouds are out to sea make sure you drive across the golden gate and visit here. The hillside has old fortifications leftover from WW2 which are fun to explore. I could have spent all day here sunning on a warm day. This is an absolute must see location if you are visiting the region.</review>

< review>
Is it possible to give negative stars? I can't put into words just how badly this place ruined our night. I was in charge of feeding 54 high school boys after a football game. I called the day before to order the pizzas. I should have known there might be a problem when the girl taking my order said I should place the order the day of the event, "in case the order gets lost." The other mom I was doing the meals with called Friday at 4pm to place the order. 54 large pizzas. Nice size order wouldn't you think? We planned on picking up the order at 8:30 pm. They said not a problem. She wanted to pay over the phone. They said, no, pay when you pick up. We thought that was weird. Why would you start making 54 pizzas without the assurance that the person would be there to pick up the order? Nevertheless, we thought all was fine. We get there at 8:30pm and say we are here for the 54 pizzas. They looked at each other, and just went, ohhh...did you do it? No, did you do it? We had maybe an hour tops to figure something out. These are big junior and senior high school football players. THAT WE FEED A MEAL TO! We saw Taco Bell across the street, and we run there, and thankfully, they were able to help us. And if you are reading this, thinking you want to order numerous pizzas from this Little Caesars, please consider going to the Taco Bell for their Party Box. I am writing my rave review for them next. And the boys LOVED it!< /review>

<Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Great food, great service. Fast service too considering I went during the dinner rush hour. It seems a bit pricey at first but the food is definitely worth it! Tons of options and a few unique burgers too. I believe they also have vegetarian burgers as well which is a nice inclusion to have for vegetarian people.
Outdoor dining during Covid is nice although it can feel a little cramped but definitely one of the better restaurants to go to during this time. They have a firm grip on the situation and have barriers between tables as well which I haven't seen in many other places.<//Text>

<user_name>Richie Zeng<//user_name>< Review>
This is my go-to place whenever we have people visiting Berkeley and want to get a large group together to eat. They always seem to have just enough space to fit our group, ranging anywhere from 4-10.

They have a great selection of burgers, all of them great. My personal favorites are Maui Waui, Baja, and Hickory.

The fries are delicious and come in huge portions. We usually get a full size serving of fries to split. The only fries I wouldn't recommend are the truffle fries. You can smell the truffle oil, but it doesn't really impact the taste, especially if you're going to be dipping them in ketchup.

Really generous portions. Expect to be stuffed by the time you're through with your burger and fries. If you get a shake in on top of that...well, good luck. I still feel full by the time I should be eating my next meal.< /Review>

<UserId.>101229155541175109091< /UserId.>< username>
Lesther Papa<//username>
<time>1568685622250</time>< rate>
5< /rate>
< review>
We got to the restaurant and it's pretty amazing! There is a great patio area and in the restaurant is cozy with wood furniture and a fireplace. There isn't a lot of street parking in this area but there is a Safeway right across the street.

The servers were really attentive to our needs and were really quick at taking our order. Food came out super quick. We ordered curly fries, the Big Barney, and the Voodoo Burger. The fries were on our table in less than 10 minutes and the our burgers were there in another 10 minutes. The fries were super fresh and hot. The ranch they have for it seems homemade and pairs well with the fries. Our burgers were hot and juicy. I would have liked my bun to be toasted and the pattie to be more heavily seasoned but it was still an excellent burger and nothing a salt shaker and pepper grinder could not fix (they were already there on the table along with ketchup, mustard, Dijon, and Tabasco).

Overall we had an excellent experience and I'm sure we'll be back soon.<//review>

<Pics>None< /Pics>< text>
This was one of the best burgers I've ever eaten. I got the Gastropub Burger, a 1/2 lb of Certified Angus Beef cooked medium, served on a pretzel bun and topped with provolone, bacon (perfectly cooked and flavored), a fried egg, and blackened potato chips. It was as red, juicy, and flavorful as you could wish. The steak fries were the Platonic ideal of steak fries. The chocolate milkshake (served with a spoon and with the extra in a blender cup, like it should be) was thick and rich. The atmosphere - wood tables and beams, with a roaring fire - was warm and comfortable, and the staff were smiling and hospitable. This place is exactly what a gourmet burger restaurant should be.</text>

Best onion rings and fries ever. I would come back to this place just for their onion rings. The rings come in the size of your fist, full of flavors and requires couple bites to consume these goodies. The hamburgers are not bad, but onion rings and fries are the must haves.

<Rate>5< /Rate><Date>1483177173099< /Date>< review>
Quickie:
+ Lived in North Berkeley for 3 years during college and only one block away from the Gourmet Ghetto - so to say I frequented Barney's is an understatement.
+ Friggin' amazing burgers

---

Food:
What can I say? The burgers are delicious as are their fries (both steak cut and sweet potato). It's hard to narrow down but I think the French burger is my favorite (Crumbled Bleu cheese and bacon, yum). But in the number of times I've been there, I've probably tried over half the menu and my friends accounted for the rest. Always spectacular, very different combinations - just an all-around nice burger joint.

Overall:
They do take-out. as well, so if you have a midterm to cram for back at home, just call in and pick up in 15. All in all, Barney's is a great alternative to a greasy fast food burger - they do gourmet on a broke college kid's budget.<//review>
